List of space groups and symmetry elements for the program MoloVol.
https://github.com/jmaglic/MoloVol
File version: 2021-07-09

###############################################################################
Notes: 
X Y Z correspond to unit cell axes.
x y z correspond to atom coordinates in the X Y Z coordinate system. 
These values should not be confused with cartesian coordinates.

The space group names H-M provided in this file correspond to the short Hermannâ€“Mauguin notation.
The H-M notations provided in this file use only upper case letters and comprise no blank space.
The H-M notations provided in this file are compatible with cif and pdb files with some exceptions:
For space groups 146,148,155,160,161,166,167:
	the H-M notations follow the PDB format replacing 'R' with 'H' in the hexagonal setting
	and is thus not compatible with cif files.
For space groups 48,50,59,68,70,85,86,88,125,126,129,130,133,134,137,138,141,142,201,203,222,224,227,228:
	the H-M notations for the alternative origin 2 setting ends with ':2' to mark the difference.
For the above groups, both settings are provided (hexagonal/rhombohedral and origin 1/origin 2).
###############################################################################

Space group #1
_symmetry_space_group_name_H-M    'P1'
_symmetry_equiv_pos_as_xyz
  x,y,z
_symmetry_equiv_pos_as_matrix Xx Xy Xz Yx Yy Yz Zx Zy Zz XX YY ZZ
1 0 0 0 1 0 0 0 1 0 0 0 
Space group end
